OBJECT Report 78860 Werkverdeling Peek Sales
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS9.00.SMART.OK;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnPreReport=BEGIN

                  Counter := 0;
                  TellCounter := 0;
                  VerkoperFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Salesperson Code");
                  TrajectFilter := "Try-out".GETFILTER(Code);
                  EstimatorFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER(Estimator);
                  ContactNoFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Contact No.");
                  AllFilters := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTERS;
                  Kostenplaatsfilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Global Dimension 1 Code");

                  //,Salesperson Code,Global Dimension 1 Code

                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                    CREATE(xlApp,FALSE,TRUE);
                    xlBook := xlApp.Workbooks.Add;
                    xlSheet := xlApp.Sheets.Add;
                    xlApp.DisplayAlerts := FALSE;
                    xlSheet.Name := FORMAT('Werkverdeling');
                    xlSheet.Select;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1:C1').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Value := 'WERKVERDELING SALES';
                    xlSheet.Range('A4').Value := 'Status';
                    xlSheet.Range('B4').Value := 'Status trajectofferte';
                    xlSheet.Range('C4').Value := 'Traject';
                    xlSheet.Range('D4').Value := 'Hoofdtraject';
                    xlSheet.Range('E4').Value := 'Calculatie';
                    xlSheet.Range('F4').Value := 'Project';
                    xlSheet.Range('G4').Value := 'Service';
                    xlSheet.Range('H4').Value := 'Omschrijving';
                    xlSheet.Range('I4').Value := 'Bestek';
                    xlSheet.Range('J4').Value := 'Type';
                    xlSheet.Range('K4').Value := 'Kostenplaats';
                    xlSheet.Range('L4').Value := 'Offerte';
                    xlSheet.Range('M4').Value := 'Klant nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range('N4').Value := 'Klant';
                    xlSheet.Range('O4').Value := 'A,B,C,D';
                    xlSheet.Range('P4').Value := 'Eindklant';
                    xlSheet.Range('Q4').Value := 'A,B,C,D';
                    xlSheet.Range('R4').Value := 'Start offerte';
                    xlSheet.Range('S4').Value := 'Aanvraagdatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('T4').Value := 'Nota van inlichtingen';
                    xlSheet.Range('U4').Value := 'Indiendatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('V4').Value := 'Aanbesteding';
                    xlSheet.Range('W4').Value := 'Verwachte orderdatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('X4').Value := 'Planning geinformeerd';
                    xlSheet.Range('Y4').Value := 'Behandelaar';
                    xlSheet.Range('Z4').Value := 'Verkoper';
                    xlSheet.Range('AA4').Value := 'Ingevoerd door';
                    xlSheet.Range('AB4').Value := 'Tellend';
                    xlSheet.Range('AC4').Value := 'Verwachte order bedrag';
                    xlSheet.Range('AD4').Value := 'Kans';
                    xlSheet.Range('AE4').Value := 'OH';
                  //xlSheet.Range('AF4').Value := 'Soort werk';
                    xlSheet.Range('AF4').Value := 'Rol Peek';
                    xlSheet.Range('AG4').Value := 'Offer Type';
                    xlSheet.Range('AH4').Value := 'Type of Work';
                    xlSheet.Range('AI4').Value := 'Category';
                    xlSheet.Range('AJ4').Value := 'Products 1';
                    xlSheet.Range('AK4').Value := 'Products 1 Amount';
                    xlSheet.Range('AL4').Value := 'Products 2'; ;
                    xlSheet.Range('AM4').Value := 'Products 2 Amount';
                    xlSheet.Range('AN4').Value := '100% offerte';
                    xlSheet.Range('AO4').Value := 'Opmerkingen';

                    xlSheet.Range('A1:AO4').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A4:AO4').Interior.ColorIndex(36);

                    RowNo := 5;
                  END;
                END;

    OnPostReport=VAR
                   TempRange@1100525000 : Text[30];
                 BEGIN

                   IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                     xlSheet.Cells.Select;
                     xlSheet.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit ;

                     TempRange := STRSUBSTNO('A4:AO%1',RowNo - 1);
                     xlSheet.Range(TempRange).AutoFilter;

                     xlApp.Range('A5').Select;
                     xlApp.ActiveWindow.FreezePanes := TRUE;

                     xlApp.Visible := TRUE;
                     ERROR('');
                   END;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;PageLoop          ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                   //FROM SECTION
                                  SHOWFOOTER :=  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Leads);
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525126;1;Column;Number_PageLoop    ;
               SourceExpr=PageLoop.Number }

    { 1100525114;1;Column;PageLoopGROUP      ;
               SourceExpr='PageLoop' }

    { 1100525113;1;Column;SHOWFOOTER         ;
               SourceExpr=SHOWFOOTER }

    { 1100525006;1;Column;COMPANYNAME_ExtensionContract;
               SourceExpr=COMPANYNAME }

    { 1100525007;1;Column;FORMATTODAY_ExtensionContract;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(CURRENTDATETIME) }

    { 1100525111;1;Column;Counter_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=Counter }

    { 1100525112;1;Column;TellCounter_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=TellCounter }

    { 1100525001;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012758;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                                CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimator,Contact No.,Salesperson Code,Global Dimension 1 Code,Leading }

    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012750;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               LastFieldNo := FIELDNO(Code);
                               CheckTryOutQuotes;

                               IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND
                                  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Leads)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF Kostenplaatsfilter <> '' THEN
                                 SETFILTER("Global Dimension 1 Code",Kostenplaatsfilter);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN


                                  IF NOT Uitgebreid AND
                                    ("Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout" = "Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout"::Main)
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER(Leading) <> '' THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF "Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET("Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;
                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(Status,1,3);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(Code);
                                  Change := CheckChance(Code);

                                  IF "Expected Order Date" < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum      := "Expected Order Date";
                                    "Expected Order Date" := 0D;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum      := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", "Try-out".Code);

                                  PrintTryOut := (NOT TryOutQuote.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE)) AND
                                                 (Status <= 'T70'                      );

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1 THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  // (Uitgebreid) AND (Status = 'T00  LEAD') THEN BEGIN
                                  IF (Uitgebreid) AND (PrintTryOut) THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 41 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value :=  TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value :=  Code;
                                    IF "Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout" <> "Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout"::Single THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := "Try-out"."Main Try-out"; // FORMAT("Single/Main/Sub Tryout");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value :=  Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Lead';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT("Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF "Expected Order Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := "Expected Order Date";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value :=  NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := "Order Amount (LCY)";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value :=  FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(Code,TRUE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION
                                  SHOWTryOut1 := ((NOT Uitgebreid) AND ((FilterOpt = FilterOpt::Leads) OR (FilterOpt = FilterOpt::Alles)));

                                  //`CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(Status = 'T00  LEAD');
                                  SHOWTryOut2 := ((NOT Uitgebreid) AND (PrintTryOut) AND
                                    ((FilterOpt = FilterOpt::Leads) OR (FilterOpt = FilterOpt::Alles)))
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Code }

    { 1100525116;2;Column;SHOWTryOut1        ;
               SourceExpr=SHOWTryOut1 }

    { 1100525115;2;Column;SHOWTryOut2        ;
               SourceExpr=SHOWTryOut2 }

    { 1100525047;2;Column;TryOutGROUP        ;
               SourceExpr='TryOut' }

    { 1100525008;2;Column;TrajectStatus_TryOut;
               SourceExpr=TrajectStatus }

    { 1100525009;2;Column;Code_TryOut        ;
               SourceExpr=Code }

    { 1100525010;2;Column;Description_TryOut ;
               SourceExpr=Description }

    { 1100525011;2;Column;NaamEindklant_TryOut;
               SourceExpr=NaamEindklant }

    { 1100525012;2;Column;CheckABCDNrEindklant_TryOut;
               SourceExpr=CheckABCD(NrEindklant) }

    { 1100525013;2;Column;BoldVerwOrdDatum_TryOut;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(BoldVerwOrdDatum) }

    { 1100525014;2;Column;ExpectedOrderDate_TryOut;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT("Expected Order Date") }

    { 1100525015;2;Column;NaamVerkoper_TryOut;
               SourceExpr=NaamVerkoper }

    { 1100525016;2;Column;OrderAmount_TryOut ;
               SourceExpr="Order Amount (LCY)" }

    { 1100525017;2;Column;Change_TryOut      ;
               SourceExpr=Change }

    { 1100525003;1;DataItem;Toewijzen        ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND
                                  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::"Aanvragen toe te wijzen")
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.RESET;
                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF EstimatorFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.SETFILTER(Estimator,EstimatorFilter);
                               IF ContactNoFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.SETFILTER("Contact No.",ContactNoFilter);

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  Tellend := FALSE;
                                  TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
                                  Ingpepland := '';
                                  EHD := '';
                                  EstimateStr := '';
                                  BoldIndienDatum := 0D;
                                  BoldAanbestDatum := 0D;
                                  NaamVerkoper := '';
                                  Behandelaar := '';

                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus := COPYSTR(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.");

                                  IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar := GetBehandelaar(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Estimator);
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtTrajectbedrag(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                  Tellend := CheckLeadingOffer(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                  IF Tellend THEN
                                    TellCounter += 1;
                                  Change := CheckChance(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                  Onderhoud := CheckOnderhoud(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.");
                                  Ingpepland := CheckIngepland(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                  EHD := CheckEHD(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr := CheckEstimateNo(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.");
                                  SoortWerk := CheckSoortwerk(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                  RolPeek := CheckRolPeek(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);

                                  IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF Tellend AND (TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1) THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  IF Tellend AND (TrajectStatus <> TrjectOffStatus) THEN
                                    TrajectStatus := TrajectStatus + ' !';

                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 41 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.",TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                    IF MultiProj THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Try-out No.",TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Tender No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Aanvraag toe te wijzen';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Creation Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Creation Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Apply Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Apply Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Assign Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Register Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Register Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Ja' + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := RolPeek;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckOfferType(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,'Products 1');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := CheckFeatureDec(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,'Products 1');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := CheckFeatureDec(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,'Products 2');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,'100% offerte');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(TempAanvragenToeteWijzen.Code,FALSE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF TrjectOffStatus <= 'T10' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldIndienDatum := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Register Date";
                                      TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Register Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;

                                    IF TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldAanbestDatum := TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Tender Date";
                                      TempAanvragenToeteWijzen."Tender Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;
                                  IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
                                    IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION
                                  SHOWToewijzen1  := (NOT Uitgebreid);
                                  SHOWToewijzen2  := ((NOT Uitgebreid) AND (TrajectStatus < 'T30'));
                                  SHOWToewijzen3  := ((NOT Uitgebreid) AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30'));
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525119;2;Column;SHOWToewijzen1     ;

    { 1100525045;2;Column;CheckOfferTypeTempAanvragenToeteWijzenCode_Toewijzen;

    { 1100525046;2;Column;CheckTypeOfWorkTempAanvragenToeteWijzenCode_Toewijzen;

    { 1100525004;1;DataItem;Aanvragen        ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND
                                  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Aanvragen)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               TempAanvragen.RESET;
                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragen.SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF EstimatorFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragen.SETFILTER(Estimator,EstimatorFilter);
                               IF ContactNoFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragen.SETFILTER("Contact No.",ContactNoFilter);

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempAanvragen.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempAanvragen.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempAanvragen.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  TempAanvragen.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
                                  Tellend := FALSE;
                                  Ingpepland := '';
                                  EHD := '';
                                  EstimateStr := '';
                                  BoldIndienDatum := 0D;
                                  BoldAanbestDatum := 0D;
                                  NaamVerkoper := '';
                                  Behandelaar := '';

                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(TempAanvragen."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus := COPYSTR(TempAanvragen.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(TempAanvragen."Try-out No.");

                                  IF TempAanvragen.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar := GetBehandelaar(TempAanvragen.Estimator);
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtTrajectbedrag(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                  Tellend := CheckLeadingOffer(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                  IF Tellend THEN
                                    TellCounter += 1;
                                  Change := CheckChance(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                  Onderhoud := CheckOnderhoud(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(TempAanvragen."Try-out No.");
                                  Ingpepland := CheckIngepland(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                  EHD := CheckEHD(TempAanvragen."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr := CheckEstimateNo(TempAanvragen.Code,TempAanvragen."Try-out No.");
                                  SoortWerk := CheckSoortwerk(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                  RolPeek := CheckRolPeek(TempAanvragen.Code);

                                  IF TempAanvragen."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(TempAanvragen."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  IF Tellend AND (TrajectStatus <> TrjectOffStatus) THEN
                                    TrajectStatus := TrajectStatus + ' !';

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", TempAanvragen."Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF Tellend AND (TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1) THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 41 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempAanvragen."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(TempAanvragen."Try-out No.",TempAanvragen.Code);
                                    IF MultiProj THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(TempAanvragen."Try-out No.",TempAanvragen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := TempAanvragen.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := TempAanvragen."Tender No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Aanvraag';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := TempAanvragen."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := TempAanvragen.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TempAanvragen."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := TempAanvragen."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(TempAanvragen."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF TempAanvragen."Creation Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := TempAanvragen."Creation Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragen."Apply Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := TempAanvragen."Apply Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragen."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := TempAanvragen."Assign Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragen."Register Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := TempAanvragen."Register Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragen."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := TempAanvragen."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := TempAanvragen."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Ja'  + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := RolPeek;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckOfferType(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(TempAanvragen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragen.Code,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragen.Code,'Products 1' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := CheckFeatureDec(TempAanvragen.Code,'Products 1' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragen.Code,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := CheckFeatureDec(TempAanvragen.Code,'Products 2' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := CheckFeature(TempAanvragen.Code,'100% offerte');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(TempAanvragen.Code,FALSE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF TrjectOffStatus <= 'T10' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF TempAanvragen."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldIndienDatum               := TempAanvragen."Register Date";
                                      TempAanvragen."Register Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;

                                    IF TempAanvragen."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldAanbestDatum            := TempAanvragen."Tender Date";
                                      TempAanvragen."Tender Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
                                    IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  IF Uitgebreid AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30') THEN BEGIN
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END;


                                  //FROM SECTION
                                  SHOWAanvragen1 := (NOT Uitgebreid);
                                  SHOWAanvragen2 := ((NOT Uitgebreid) AND (TrajectStatus < 'T30'));
                                  SHOWAanvragen3 := ((NOT Uitgebreid) AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30'));
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE CheckTryOutQuotes@1000000017();
    VAR
      TryOutQuote@1000000000 : Record 11012758;
      TryOut@1000000001 : Record 11012750;
    BEGIN
      IF AllFilters <>'' THEN
        TryOutQuote.COPYFILTERS("Try-out Quote");
      IF TrajectFilter <> '' THEN
        TryOutQuote.SETFILTER("Try-out No.",TrajectFilter);
      IF TryOutQuote.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF (TryOut.GET(TryOutQuote."Try-out No.")) AND
           (TryOut."Single/Main/Sub Tryout" = TryOut."Single/Main/Sub Tryout"::Main)
        THEN
          EXIT;
        REPEAT
          CASE TryOutQuote.Status OF
            //Toe te wijzen
            'T03  ASSIGN':FillTempAanvragenToeteWijzen(TryOutQuote);
            'T04  ASSIGN':FillTempAanvragenToeteWijzen(TryOutQuote);
            '': FillTempAanvragenToeteWijzen(TryOutQuote);
            //Aanvragen
            'T01  TASK'  :FillTempAanvragen(TryOutQuote);
            'T05  BUDGET':FillTempAanvragen(TryOutQuote);
            'T10  OFFER' :FillTempAanvragen(TryOutQuote);
            //Uitgebrachte offertes
            'T15  BUDGET SENT':FillTempuitgebrachteoffertes(TryOutQuote);
            'T20  OFFER SENT' :FillTempuitgebrachteoffertes(TryOutQuote);
            //Hold
            'T12  ON HOLD': BEGIN END; //SKIP
            ELSE IF (COPYSTR(FORMAT(TryOutQuote.Status), 1, 3) >= 'T01') AND
                    (COPYSTR(FORMAT(TryOutQuote.Status), 1, 3) <= 'T24')
                 THEN
                   FillTempuitgebrachteoffertes(TryOutQuote);
          END;
        UNTIL TryOutQuote.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckProjectNo@1000000142(tryout@1000000001 : Code[20];tryoutquote@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000000 : Record 11012761;
    BEGIN
      MultiProj := FALSE;
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",tryout);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",tryoutquote);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Project No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
          MultiProj := TRUE;
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
          EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Project No.");
      END ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckServiceNo@1000000143(tryout@1000000001 : Code[20];tryoutquote@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000000 : Record 11012761;
    BEGIN
      MultiServ := FALSE;
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",tryout);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",tryoutquote);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Order No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
          MultiServ := TRUE;
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
          EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Order No.");
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Service Order No.");
        TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Contract No.",'<>%1','');
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
            MultiServ := TRUE;
          IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Contract No.");
        END ELSE BEGIN
          TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.");
          TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Location No.",'<>%1','');
          IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
              MultiServ := TRUE;
            IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
              EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Location No.");
          END ELSE
            EXIT('');
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetCommentLines@1000000004(Code@1000000000 : Code[20];Traject@1000000001 : Boolean) : Text[500];
    VAR
      CommentLineRec@1000000002 : Record 97;
      TempText@1000000003 : Text[500];
    BEGIN
      IF Traject THEN
        CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::"Try-out")
      ELSE
        CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::"Try-out Quote");

      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("No.", Code);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF TempText = '' THEN
            TempText := CommentLineRec.Comment
          ELSE
            TempText := TempText + ' - ' + CommentLineRec.Comment;
        UNTIL CommentLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EXIT(TempText);
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
